[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `json_fuzz` harness in the Shadowsocks codebase. The overflow occurs in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `json_parse_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/shadowsocks/src/json.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when parsing JSON input, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting in a one-byte read beyond an allocated heap buffer.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer executed the entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `json_fuzz.c`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich calls into the JSON parser in `json_parse_ex`. AddressSanitizer reported a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone-byte read past the end of an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte heap allocation.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is classified as a heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The read occurs at address [0m[1;36m0x5020000000b8[0m[39m, exactly one byte beyond an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion allocated via `malloc`.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack trace identifies `json_parse_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m634[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as the immediate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msite of the invalid memory access, and `json_parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m958[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as the caller.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The heap allocation originates from the fuzzer driver code when setting up the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput buffer passed to the parser.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The vulnerable code is exercised by the fuzzing harness but the harness itself [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis not the root cause—rather it exposes the out-of-bounds access in the parser [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```  [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min order to prevent reads beyond the buffer. However, after applying this change, [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimple comparison adjustment did not eliminate the out-of-bounds access.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen `state.ptr` reaches or exceeds `end`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        json_char b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr >= end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : *state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow was triggered in the JSON parser [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`json_parse_ex` in src/json.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when running the `json_fuzz` fuzzer. The overflow [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs due to reading one byte past the end of the input buffer. A patch was [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempted that adds explicit boundary checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mby comparing `state.ptr` against [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`end`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before each byte read and reorganizes several `if` conditions for unicode [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape processing. However, applying this patch led to a slew of compilation [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors, including misleading indentation warnings, “default” labels outside of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mswitches, and numerous uses of an undeclared variable `b`.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer: `json_fuzz` using libFuzzer with [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m iterations on a single input.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Crash type: AddressSanitizer reports a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte heap-buffer-overflow at address [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b8[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Faulty location: `json_parse_ex` in `src/shadowsocks/src/json.c` at line [0m[1;36m634[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcolumn [0m[1;36m55[0m[39m.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Backtrace highlights:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `json_parse_ex` reading `*state.ptr` when `state.ptr == end`.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Called by `json_parse`, then `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, then the libFuzzer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruntime.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allocation that was overflowed: an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte region, immediately followed by the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget byte.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observation: the parser loop uses `json_char b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr == end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` but later code branches still do `*++state.ptr` without verifying [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msufficient remaining bytes.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe submitted patch makes two primary changes in `src/json.c`:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **General byte-read fix**  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Original:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     json_char b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr == end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : *state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Patched:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* prevent reading one byte past buffer end *[0m[35m/[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     json_char b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr >= end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : *state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Unicode escape sequence checks**  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replaces checks like:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b1 = [0m[1;35mhex_value[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         … [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m goto e_failed; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With a combined `if`-expression using pointer arithmetic:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* need at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes before advancing *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         state.ptr + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m > end ||[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b1 = [0m[1;35mhex_value[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         …[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe shadowsocks JSON parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`json_parse_ex`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was crashing under fuzzing with an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow when reading one byte past the end of its [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput buffer. A patch was attempted in `src/json.c` to tighten bounds checks in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmain parsing loop and in Unicode escape handling:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changed the primary byte‐fetch expression from `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr == end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr >= end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : *state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Added explicit checks that ensure four extra bytes exist before reading a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\uXXXX` escape and six extra bytes for surrogate pairs.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying this patch, the fuzzer still triggers the same kind of heap buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow in the same function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnow reported at a slightly shifted line number[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating the overflow remains unaddressed.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During `json_fuzz` execution under AddressSanitizer, the parser read one byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m‐byte allocation.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash occurs in `json_parse_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m634[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during string parsing, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically when handling escape sequences and advancing `state.ptr`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer log shows `READ of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at [0m[1;36m0x[0m[39m…0b8`, exactly at the end of the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x[0m[39m…0b0,[0m[1;36m0x[0m[39m…0b8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace highlights calls through `json_parse`, `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand into the libFuzzer harness.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parser’s main loop increments `state.ptr` unconditionally and only checks [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`== end` before dereferencing.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unicode escape [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\uXXXX`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m logic assumes at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m subsequent bytes are [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent; surrogate‐pair logic assumes [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow happens despite these assumptions, so some pointer advance path [0m  [2m                [0m
